<think> Clearly, we are dealing with the numbers 84, 18, and 3. Let's start by looking at each number and thinking about how to combine them to approach 30.
Given that 30 is very close to 84/2, it could mean we should consider division in the formulation.
Multiplying 18 and 3 would give us 54, much larger than 30, so let's skip that for now.
Using 18 and dividing by 3 obviously gives us 6, not what we need.
Now remember 84 is the largest number, so we should think about subtracting smaller numbers from 84 to reach closer to our answer.
Subtracting 18 from 84 gives us 66, and dividing this by 3 would give us:
66 / 3 = 22, still not 30.
To get closer to 30, we should try subtracting 18 from another large number and see where that gets us:
(84 - 18) / 3 = 66 / 3 = 22.
Clearly, 22 is too far from our target of 30, so we need to try using 18 in a different way.
Now, let's consider using the numbers in a different order and think about subtraction and multiplication:
Try 18 * 3 = 54 and then subtract 24 from 84. We need to find a number that when subtracted from 84 gives 30.
84 - 54 = 30. So if we do 84 - (18 * 3), we get 30.
There we go! That's the equation we are looking for.</think>
<answer> (84 - (18 * 3)) </answer>

75 - 38 = 37, but we need 73, so this isn't the answer.
Considering division operations, 75 / 18 or 75 / 20 won't get us 73.
Adding 75 and 20 doesn't help (75 + 20 = 95, not 73).
Finally, subtracting: 75 - 20 = 55. To get to 73 from 55, we need to reduce 55 by 22, which isn't an immediate possibility.
Considering the nature of the problem, it appears that the sought equation is a combination involving the subtraction of 20 from 75 and then adding something that equals 73 when added to 55.
75 - 20 = 55. To reach 73, we need to add 18 (because 55 + 18 = 73).
So the equation is: 75 - 20 + 18 = 73.
</think>
<answer> 75 - 20 + 18 </answer>

Considering 28 - 43 = -15, we went wrong with that approach. I need to find a way to rearrange. 28 - 43 is negative, so using 68 will reverse the sign, aiming for 43 - 28 = 15, which is close to 11.
Therefore, (68 - 43) - (28 - 41) = 25 - 11 = 14, which got me a bit off. However, I look for 11 further in my options.

Since this doesn't work, let's try another approach: if we can make 38 - 11 = 27, we could then use 64 + 33 = 97, and then 97 - 27 = 70.
Checking, 38 - 11 = 27, and 64 + 33 = 97. Now we have 97 - 27 = 70, which works.
</think>
<answer> (64 + 33) - (38 - 11) </answer>

Now, if we take 11 from 64, we get 53. This makes 65 - 11 = 54.
So, 54 + 16 = 70.
Since 16 is the same as 38 - 22, and knowing 22 can be formed from 33 - 11, the equation can be written as follows:
(38 - (33 - 11)) + (64 - 11) = 70
We can simplify this to: 38 - 33 + 11 + 64 - 11 = 70
Now, combining like terms: (38 + 11 + 64) - (33 + 11) = 113 - 44 = 70.
But again, there's a simpler way to express it using addition and subtraction directly: (64 + 11) - (38 - 33) = 70.
Thus, the equation becomes: 64 + 11 - (38 - 33) = 70
</think>
<answer> 64 + 11 - (38 - 33) </answer>

One approach is to try to subtract or add numbers to reach 29.
If we subtract 21 from 56, we get 35. Then, to get to 29 from 35 by using the last number 48, we would need to perform 35 - 48 + x = 29.
However, since such a straightforward operation doesn't exist, let's consider multiplying or dividing.
Multiplying 56 by 21 gives a very large number (1176), which is too big. Dividing 56 by 21 also doesn't simplify easily.

A more promising path is to add 48 + 56 - 21. If I do this, I get:
48 + 56 = 104
Then, 104 - 21 = 83.
This is not right either.
Given the constraints, let's try reordering. If we take 56 - 21, which gives 35, and now subtract 48 from that:
56 - 21 = 35
35 - 48 = -13
No luck there.
Let's look at 21 + 48 = 69, then subtract 56:
21 + 48 = 69
69 - 56 = 13
Still not 29.
Another trial is to take 48 + 21 = 69, then subtract 56:
48 + 21 = 69
69 - 56 = 13
This is incorrect too.
Given the problems with trial and error, perhaps a different combination will cover all entries in our set without introducing negative values:
1. Start with 56
2. Add 21: 56 + 21 = 77
3. Subtract 48: 77 - 48 = 29
</think>
<answer> 56 + 21 - 48 </answer>

- Another try: 66 - 20 = 46, and then 46 + 9 = 55, which is exactly what we need.
So, the equation is 66 - 20 + 9 = 55.
</think>
<answer> 66 - 20 + 9 </answer>
